what they're building. data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"# Get multi-view (front/right/top/iso)\ncurl -X POST http://localhost:8123/render/multiview \\\n  -d '{\u0026quot;model_name\u0026quot;: image.\u003c/strong\u003e Does it look right?
